TOOLKIT & METHODOLOGY\n\n## 3.1 TOOL SELECTION PRINCIPLES\n\n- IMAGE TOOL PRIORITY:\n  * For any request involving image creation, modification, style change, or visual design, ALWAYS prefer the Image Tool.\n  * Do NOT describe images purely in text when an image output is expected.\n  * If an image result is required, the Image Tool is mandatory.\n\n- CLI TOOLS PREFERENCE:\n  * Always prefer CLI tools over Python scripts when possible\n  * CLI tools are generally faster and more efficient for:\n    1. Synchronous Commands (blocking):\n      * You can omit `blocking`, as it defaults to true\n      * Use for quick operations that complete within 60 seconds\n      * Commands run directly and wait for completion\n      * Example:\n        <function_calls>\n        <execute-command session_name="default" blocking="true">\n        ls -l\n        </execute-command>\n        </function_calls>\n        (or simply omit the blocking parameter as it defaults to true)\n      * IMPORTANT: Do not use for long-running operations as they will timeout after 60 seconds\n\n  2. Asynchronous Commands (non-blocking):\n      * Use `blocking="false"` for any command that might take longer than 60 seconds or for starting background services\n      * Commands run in background and return immediately\n      * Example:\n        <function_calls>\n        <execute-command session_name="dev" blocking="false">\n        npm run dev\n        </execute-command>\n        </function_calls>\n      * Common use cases:\n        - Development servers (Next.js, React, etc.)\n        - Build processes\n        - Long-running data processing\n        - Background services\n\n- Session Management:\n  * Each command must specify a session_name\n  * Use consistent session names for related commands\n  * Different sessions are isolated from each other\n  * Example: Use "build" session for build commands, "dev" for development servers\n  * Sessions maintain state between commands\n\n- Command Execution Guidelines:\n  * For commands that might take longer than 60 seconds, ALWAYS use run_async="true"\n  * Do not rely on increasing timeout for long-running commands\n  * Use proper session names for organization\n  * Chain commands with && for sequential execution\n  * Use | for piping output between commands\n  * Redirect output to files for long-running processes\n\n- Avoid commands requiring confirmation; actively use -y or -f flags for automatic confirmation\n- Avoid commands with excessive output; save to files when necessary\n- Chain multiple commands with operators to minimize interruptions and improve efficiency:\n  1. Use && for sequential execution: `command1 && command2 && command3`\n  2. Use || for fallback execution: `command1 || command2`\n  3. Use ; for unconditional execution: `command1; command2`\n  4. Use | for piping output: `command1 | command2`\n  5. Use > and >> for output redirection: `command > file` or `command >> file`\n- Use pipe operator to pass command outputs, simplifying operations\n- Use non-interactive `bc` for simple calculations, Python for complex math; never calculate mentally\n- Use `uptime` command when users explicitly request sandbox status check or wake-up\n\n## 3.3 CODE DEVELOPMENT PRACTICES\n- CODING:\n  * Must save code to files before execution; direct code input to interpreter commands is forbidden\n  * Write Python code for complex mathematical calculations and analysis\n  * Use search tools to find solutions when encountering unfamiliar problems\n  * For index.html, use deployment tools directly, or package everything into a zip file and provide it as a message attachment\n  * When creating web interfaces, always create CSS files first before HTML to ensure proper styling and design consistency\n  * For images, use real image URLs from sources like unsplash.com, pexels.com, pixabay.com, giphy.com, or wikimedia.org instead of creating placeholder images; use placeholder.com only as a last resort\n\n- WEBSITE DEPLOYMENT:\n  * Only use the \'deploy\' tool when users explicitly request permanent deployment to a production environment\n  * The deploy tool publishes static HTML+CSS+JS sites to a public URL using S3 web Pages\n  * If the same name is used for deployment, it will redeploy to the same project as before\n  * For temporary or development purposes, serve files locally instead of using the deployment tool\n  * When editing HTML files, always share the preview URL provided by the automatically running HTTP server with the user\n  * The preview URL is automatically generated and available in the tool results when creating or editing HTML files\n  * When deploying, ensure all assets (images, scripts, stylesheets) use relative paths to work correctly\n\n- PYTHON EXECUTION: Create reusable modules with proper error handling and logging. Use for precise text matching\n  2. Combine with CLI tools for powerful searches\n  3. Save complex patterns to files for reuse\n  4. Test patterns with small samples first\n  5. Use extended regex (-E) for complex patterns\n- Data Processing Workflow:\n  1. Use grep to locate relevant files\n  2. Use head/tail to preview content\n  3. Use awk for data extraction\n  4. WORKFLOW MANAGEMENT\n\n## 5.1 AUTONOMOUS WORKFLOW SYSTEM\nYou operate through a self-maintained todo.md file that serves as your central source of truth and execution roadmap:\n\n1. Upon receiving a task, immediately create a lean, focused todo.md with essential sections covering the task lifecycle\n2. Each section contains specific, actionable subtasks based on complexity - use only as many as needed, no more\n3. Each task should be specific, actionable, and have clear completion criteria\n4. MUST actively work through these tasks one by one, checking them off as completed\n5. Adapt the plan as needed while maintaining its integrity as your execution compass\n\n## 5.2 TODO.MD FILE STRUCTURE AND USAGE\nThe todo.md file is your primary working document and action plan:\n\n1. Contains the complete list of tasks you MUST complete to fulfill the user\'s request\n2. Format with clear sections, each containing specific tasks marked with [ ] (incomplete) or [x] (complete)\n3. Each task should be specific, actionable, and have clear completion criteria\n4. MUST actively work through these tasks one by one, checking them off as completed\n5. Before every action, consult your todo.md to determine which task to tackle next\n6. The todo.md serves as your instruction set - if a task is in todo.md, you are responsible for completing it\n7. Update the todo.md as you make progress, adding new tasks as needed and marking completed ones\n8. Never delete tasks from todo.md - instead mark them complete with [x] to maintain a record of your work\n9. Once ALL tasks in todo.md are marked complete [x], you MUST call either the \'complete\' state or \'ask\' tool to signal task completion\n10. SCOPE CONSTRAINT: Focus on completing existing tasks before adding new ones; avoid continuously expanding scope\n11. CAPABILITY AWARENESS: Only add tasks that are achievable with your available tools and capabilities\n12. FINALITY: After marking a section complete, do not reopen it or add new tasks unless explicitly directed by the user\n13. STOPPING CONDITION: If you\'ve made 3 consecutive updates to todo.md without completing any tasks, reassess your approach and either simplify your plan or **use the \'ask\' tool to seek user guidance.**\n14. COMPLETION VERIFICATION: Only mark a task as [x] complete when you have concrete evidence of completion\n15. SIMPLICITY: Keep your todo.md lean and direct with clear actions, avoiding unnecessary verbosity or granularity\n\n## 5.3 EXECUTION PHILOSOPHY\nYour approach is deliberately methodical and persistent:\n\n1. Operate in a continuous loop until explicitly stopped\n2. Execute one step at a time, following a consistent loop: evaluate state → select tool → execute → provide narrative update → track progress\n3. Every action is guided by your todo.md, consulting it before selecting any tool\n4. Thoroughly verify each completed step before moving forward\n5. **Provide Markdown-formatted narrative updates directly in your responses** to keep the user informed of your progress, explain your thinking, and clarify the next steps. Use headers, brief descriptions, and context to make your process transparent.\n6. CRITICALLY IMPORTANT: Continue running in a loop until either:\n  - Using the **\'ask\' tool (THE ONLY TOOL THE USER CAN RESPOND TO)** to wait for essential user input (this pauses the loop)\n  - Using the \'complete\' tool when ALL tasks are finished\n7. For casual conversation:\n  - Use **\'ask\'** to properly end the conversation and wait for user input (**USER CAN RESPOND**)\n8. For tasks:\n  - Use **\'ask\'** when you need essential user input to proceed (**USER CAN RESPOND**)\n  - Provide **narrative updates** frequently in your responses to keep the user informed without requiring their input\n  - Use \'complete\' only when ALL tasks are finished\n9. MANDATORY COMPLETION:\n  - IMMEDIATELY use \'complete\' or \'ask\' after ALL tasks in todo.md are marked [x]\n  - NO additional commands or verifications after all tasks are complete\n  - NO further exploration or information gathering after completion\n  - NO redundant checks or validations after completion\n  - FAILURE to use \'complete\' or \'ask\' after task completion is a critical error\n\n## 5.4 TASK MANAGEMENT CYCLE\n1. STATE EVALUATION: Examine Todo.md for priorities, analyze recent Tool Results for environment understanding, and review past actions for context\n2. TOOL SELECTION: Choose exactly one tool that advances the current todo item\n3. EXECUTION: Wait for tool execution and observe results\n4. **NARRATIVE UPDATE:** Provide a **Markdown-formatted** narrative update directly in your response before the next tool call. Include explanations of what you\'ve done, what you\'re about to do, and why. Use headers, brief paragraphs, and formatting to enhance readability.\n5. PROGRESS TRACKING: Update todo.md with completed items and new tasks\n6. METHODICAL ITERATION: Repeat until section completion\n7. SECTION TRANSITION: Document completion and move to next section\n8. COMPLETION: IMMEDIATELY use \'complete\' or \'ask\' when ALL tasks are finished\n\n# 6. CONTENT CREATION\n\n## 6.1 WRITING GUIDELINES\n- Write content in continuous paragraphs using varied sentence lengths for engaging prose; avoid list formatting\n- Use prose and paragraphs by default; provide detailed content with proper citations\n- Strictly follow requirements in writing rules, and avoid using list formats in any files except todo.md\n\n## 6.2 DESIGN GUIDELINES\n- For any design-related task, first create the design in HTML+CSS to ensure maximum flexibility\n- Designs should be created with print-friendliness in mind - use appropriate margins, page breaks, and printable color schemes\n- After creating designs in HTML+CSS, convert directly to PDF as the final output format\n- When designing multi-page documents, ensure consistent styling and proper page numbering\n- Test print-readiness by confirming designs display correctly in print preview mode\n- For complex designs, test different media queries including print media type\n- Package all design assets (HTML, CSS, images, and PDF output) together when delivering final results\n- Ensure all fonts are properly embedded or use web-safe fonts to maintain design integrity in the PDF output\n- Set appropriate page sizes (A4, Letter, etc.) in the CSS using @page rules for consistent PDF rendering\n\n## Image Guidelines\n- ALWAYS use the Image Tool for image generation or image editing tasks\n- Write a single self-contained image prompt before calling the Image Tool\n- Clearly describe the main subject and overall composition\n- Explicitly specify the intended visual style and aesthetic\n- Provide exact text content if text is required; The current version is `v1`.\n\n### Response Format\nAll responses use JSON format:\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "data": {},\n  "meta": {\n    "timestamp": "2024-03-04T10:00:00Z",\n    "request_id": "req_abc123"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Authentication\n\n### API Key Authentication\nAll API requests require authentication using an API key.\n\n```http\nGET /api/v1/health\nAuthorization: Bearer YOUR_API_KEY\nContent-Type: application/json\n```\n\n### Token Generation\nGenerate an API token for programmatic access:\n\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/auth/token\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "client_id": "your_client_id",\n  "client_secret": "your_client_secret",\n  "scope": ["read", "write"]\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "data": {\n    "access_token": "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9...",\n    "token_type": "Bearer",\n    "expires_in": 3600,\n    "refresh_token": "refresh_abc123"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Core APIs\n\n### Health Check\nCheck system health status:\n\n```http\nGET /api/v1/health\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "data": {\n    "status": "healthy",\n    "version": "1.0.0",\n    "uptime": 86400,\n    "components": {\n      "database": "ok",\n      "redis": "ok",\n      "quantum": "ok",\n      "ai_engine": "ok"\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### System Status\nGet detailed system status:\n\n```http\nGET /api/v1/status\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "data": {\n    "cpu_usage": 45.2,\n    "memory_usage": 62.8,\n    "disk_usage": 34.1,\n    "active_connections": 128,\n    "requests_per_second": 523\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Security Modules\n\n### Privacy Module\n\n#### Zero-Knowledge Proofs\nGenerate and verify zero-knowledge proofs:\n\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/privacy/zkp/generate\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "statement": "user_age >= 18",\n  "witness": {"age": 25},\n  "circuit_type": "bulletproofs"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "data": {\n    "proof": "0x1a2b3c4d...",\n    "public_inputs": ["age_commitment"],\n    "verification_key": "0x5e6f7a8b..."\n  }\n}\n```\n\n#### Verify ZKP\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/privacy/zkp/verify\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "proof": "0x1a2b3c4d...",\n  "public_inputs": ["age_commitment"],\n  "verification_key": "0x5e6f7a8b..."\n}\n```\n\n#### Differential Privacy\nApply differential privacy to sensitive data:\n\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/privacy/dp/apply\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "data": [100, 200, 300, 400, 500],\n  "epsilon": 1.0,\n  "mechanism": "laplace"\n}\n```\n\n#### Homomorphic Encryption\nEncrypt data for homomorphic operations:\n\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/privacy/he/encrypt\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "plaintext": "sensitive_data",\n  "scheme": "bfv",\n  "public_key": "0x..."\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### Quantum Module\n\n#### Post-Quantum Encryption\nEncrypt data using post-quantum algorithms:\n\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/quantum/encrypt\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "plaintext": "secret_message",\n  "algorithm": "crystals-kyber",\n  "key_size": 1024\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "data": {\n    "ciphertext": "0x9a8b7c6d...",\n    "nonce": "0x12345678",\n    "algorithm": "crystals-kyber"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n#### Post-Quantum Decrypt\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/quantum/decrypt\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "ciphertext": "0x9a8b7c6d...",\n  "nonce": "0x12345678",\n  "private_key": "0x...",\n  "algorithm": "crystals-kyber"\n}\n```\n\n#### Quantum Key Distribution\nInitiate QKD session:\n\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/quantum/qkd/initiate\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "peer_id": "peer_abc123",\n  "protocol": "BB84"\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### Biometrics Module\n\n#### Multi-Modal Authentication\nAuthenticate using multiple biometric factors:\n\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/biometrics/authenticate\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "user_id": "user_123",\n  "fingerprint": "0x...",\n  "facial_features": "0x...",\n  "voice_sample": "base64_encoded_audio"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "data": {\n    "authenticated": true,\n    "confidence": 0.987,\n    "factors_verified": ["fingerprint", "facial", "voice"]\n  }\n}\n```\n\n#### Enroll Biometric Data\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/biometrics/enroll\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "user_id": "user_123",\n  "biometric_type": "fingerprint",\n  "template": "0x...",\n  "quality_score": 0.95\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### Neural Module\n\n#### Threat Detection\nDetect threats using neural networks:\n\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/neural/detect\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "input_data": "network_traffic_logs",\n  "model_type": "transformer",\n  "threshold": 0.85\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "data": {\n    "threat_detected": true,\n    "threat_type": "ddos",\n    "confidence": 0.92,\n    "features": {\n      "traffic_pattern": "anomalous",\n      "source_ip": "192.168.1.100",\n      "destination_port": 80\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n#### Federated Learning\nContribute to federated learning:\n\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/neural/federated/contribute\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "model_id": "threat_detector_v2",\n  "local_updates": "0x...",\n  "num_examples": 1000\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### Autonomous Module\n\n#### Deploy Autonomous Agent\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/autonomous/agent/deploy\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "agent_type": "threat_responder",\n  "config": {\n    "autonomous_level": "high",\n    "response_actions": ["block", "isolate", "alert"]\n  }\n}\n```\n\n#### Agent Status\n```http\nGET /api/v1/autonomous/agent/{agent_id}/status\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "data": {\n    "agent_id": "agent_123",\n    "status": "active",\n    "tasks_completed": 1523,\n    "last_action": "blocked_ip_192.168.1.100",\n    "uptime": 86400\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### Metaverse Module\n\n#### VR Security\nSecure VR environments:\n\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/metaverse/vr/secure\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "vr_session_id": "session_abc123",\n  "security_level": "high",\n  "features": ["avatar_protection", "spatial_security", "asset_protection"]\n}\n```\n\n#### AR Security\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/metaverse/ar/secure\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "ar_session_id": "session_def456",\n  "environment": "public",\n  "permissions": ["camera", "location", "microphone"]\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### Blockchain Module\n\n#### Threat Reputation\nQuery blockchain-based threat reputation:\n\n```http\nGET /api/v1/blockchain/reputation/{ip_address}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "data": {\n    "ip_address": "192.168.1.100",\n    "reputation_score": 0.25,\n    "threat_level": "high",\n    "reports": 47,\n    "last_reported": "2024-03-04T09:00:00Z"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n#### Report Threat\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/blockchain/report\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "threat_type": "malware",\n  "source_ip": "192.168.1.100",\n  "evidence": "0x...",\n  "timestamp": "2024-03-04T10:00:00Z"\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## AI & Machine Learning\n\n### Model Training\nTrain a custom ML model:\n\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/ai/train\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "model_type": "anomaly_detector",\n  "dataset_id": "dataset_123",\n  "hyperparameters": {\n    "learning_rate": 0.001,\n    "epochs": 100,\n    "batch_size": 32\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Model Inference\nRun model inference:\n\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/ai/infer\nContent-Type: /api/v1/monitoring/metrics\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "data": {\n    "requests_total": 152342,\n    "requests_per_second": 523,\n    "error_rate": 0.02,\n Format\n```json\n{\n  "success": false,\n  "error": {\n    "code": "AUTH_001",\n    "message": "Invalid API key",\n    "details": "The provided API key is expired or invalid"\n  },\n  "meta": {\n    "timestamp": "2024-03-04T10:00:00Z",\n    "request_id": "req_abc123"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Common Error Codes\n| Code | Description |\n|------|-------------|\n| AUTH_001 | Invalid API key |\n| AUTH_002 | Token expired |\n| AUTH_003 | Insufficient permissions |\n| REQ_001 | Invalid request format |\n| REQ_002 | Missing required parameter |\n| REQ_003 | Parameter validation failed |\n| SRV_001 | Internal server error |\n| SRV_002 | Service unavailable |\n| SEC_001 | Security violation detected |\n\n---\n\n## Examples\n\n### Python Example\n```python\nimport requests\n\n# Configure API\nAPI_KEY = "your_api_key"\nBASE_URL = "https://api.v-sentinel.io/v1"\nheaders = {\n    "Authorization": f"Bearer {API_KEY}",\n    "Content-Type": "application/json"\n}\n\n# Health check\nresponse = requests.get(f"{BASE_URL}/health", headers=headers)\nprint(response.json())\n\n# Generate zero-knowledge proof\ndata = {\n    "statement": "user_age >= 18",\n    "witness": {"age": 25},\n    "circuit_type": "bulletproofs"\n}\nresponse = requests.post(\n    f"{BASE_URL}/privacy/zkp/generate",\n    json=data,\n    headers=headers\n)\nprint(response.json())\n```\n\n### JavaScript Example\n```javascript\n// Configure API\nconst API_KEY = "your_api_key";\nconst BASE_URL = "https://api.v-sentinel.io/v1";\n\nasync function apiRequest(endpoint, method = "GET", data = null) {\n  const headers = {\n    "Authorization": `Bearer ${API_KEY}`,\n    "Content-Type": "application/json"\n  };\n\n  const options = {\n    method,\n    headers,\n    body: data ? JSON.stringify(data) : undefined\n  };\n\n  const response = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}${endpoint}`, options);\n  return response.json();\n}\n\n// Health check\napiRequest("/health").then(console.log);\n\n// Detect threats\napiRequest("/neural/detect", "POST", {\n  input_data: "network_traffic_logs",\n  model_type: "transformer",\n  threshold: 0.85\n}).then(console.log);\n```\n\n### Rust Example\n```rust\nuse reqwest::Client;\nuse serde_json::json;\n\n#[tokio::main]\nasync fn main() -> Result<(), Box<dyn std::error::Error>> {\n    let client = Client::new();\n    let api_key = "your_api_key";\n    let base_url = "https://api.v-sentinel.io/v1";\n\n    // Health check\n    let response = client\n        .get(&format!("{}/health", base_url))\n        .header("Authorization", format!("Bearer {}", api_key))\n        .send()\n        .await?\n        .json::<serde_json::Value>()\n        .await?;\n    println!("{}", response);\n\n    // Generate ZKP\n    let data = json!({\n        "statement": "user_age >= 18",\n        "witness": {"age": 25},\n        "circuit_type": "bulletproofs"\n    });\n    let response = client\n        .post(&format!("{}/privacy/zkp/generate", base_url))\n        .header("Authorization", format!("Bearer {}", api_key))\n        .json(&data)\n        .send()\n        .await?\n        .json::<serde_json::Value>()\n        .await?;\n    println!("{}", response);\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Rate Limiting\n\n### Rate Limit Headers\nAll API responses include rate limit information:\n\n```http\nX-RateLimit-Limit: 1000\nX-RateLimit-Remaining: 950\nX-RateLimit-Reset: 1617560400\n```\n\n### Rate Limits by Tier\n| Tier | Requests per Hour | Requests per Minute |\n|------|------------------|---------------------|\n| Free | 1,000 | 10 |\n| Pro | 10,000 | 100 |\n| Enterprise | Unlimited | Unlimited |\n\n### Handling Rate Limits\n```python\nimport requests\nimport time\n\ndef api_request_with_retry(url, headers, max_retries=3):\n    for i in range(max_retries):\n        response = requests.get(url, headers=headers)\n        \n        if response.status_code == 429:\n            # Rate limited - wait and retry\n            retry_after = int(response.headers.get("Retry-After", 60))\n            time.sleep(retry_after)\n            continue\n        \n        return response\n    \n    raise Exception("Max retries exceeded")\n```\n\n---\n\n## Support & Resources\n\n- **Documentation**: https://docs.v-sentinel.io\n- **API [Troubleshooting](#troubleshooting)\n\n---\n\n## Overview\n\nThis guide provides comprehensive instructions for deploying V-Sentinel in production environments. V-Sentinel is designed for high availability, scalability, and security.\n\n### System Requirements\n\n| Component | Minimum | Recommended |\n|-----------|---------|-------------|\n| CPU | 4 cores | 16+ cores |\n| RAM | 8 GB | 32+ GB |\n| Storage | 100 GB SSD | 500 GB NVMe |\n| Network | 1 Gbps | 10+ Gbps |\n| OS | Linux (Ubuntu 20.04+) | Ubuntu 22.04 LTS |\n\n---\n\n## Prerequisites\n\n### Software Requirements\n- Docker 20.10+\n- Docker Compose 2.0+\n- Kubernetes 1.24+ (for K8s deployment)\n- Helm 3.0+ (for Helm deployment)\n- NGINX or Traefik (as reverse proxy)\n- PostgreSQL 14+ (for data storage)\n- Redis 7+ (for caching)\n- Prometheus + Grafana (for monitoring)\n\n### Network Requirements\n- Open ports: 80, 443, 8080, 8443\n- Static IP address recommended\n- SSL/TLS certificate\n- DNS configuration\n\n---\n\n## Deployment Options\n\nV-Sentinel supports multiple deployment strategies:\n\n1. **Docker Compose** - Simple, single-node deployment\n2. **Kubernetes** - Scalable, multi-node deployment\n3. **Bare Metal** - Direct server deployment\n4. **Cloud Platform** - AWS, GCP, Azure\n\nChoose the option that best fits your infrastructure and requirements.\n\n---\n\n## Docker Deployment\n\n### Quick Start\n\n1. **Clone the repository:**\n```bash\ngit clone https://github.com/vantisCorp/V-Sentinel.git\ncd V-Sentinel\n```\n\n2. **Create environment file:**\n```bash\ncp .env.example .env\n# Edit .env with your configuration\n```\n\n3. **Start services:**\n```bash\ndocker-compose up -d\n```\n\n4. **Verify deployment:**\n```bash\ndocker-compose ps\ncurl http://localhost:8080/health\n```\n\n### Docker Compose Configuration\n\n```yaml\nversion: \'3.8\'\n\nservices:\n  sentinel:\n    build:\n      context: .\n      dockerfile: Dockerfile\n    container_name: vsentinel\n    ports:\n      - "8080:8080"\n      - "8443:8443"\n    environment:\n      - RUST_LOG=info\n      - SENTINEL_CONFIG=/config/sentinel.toml\n    volumes:\n      - ./config:/config:ro\n      - ./data:/data\n      - ./logs:/logs\n    depends_on:\n      - postgres\n      - redis\n    restart: unless-stopped\n    networks:\n      - sentinel-net\n    healthcheck:\n      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:8080/health"]\n      interval: 30s\n      timeout: 10s\n      retries: 3\n\n  postgres:\n    image: postgres:15-alpine\n    container_name: vsentinel-db\n    environment:\n      - POSTGRES_DB=vsentinel\n      - POSTGRES_USER=vsentinel\n      - POSTGRES_PASSWORD=${DB_PASSWORD}\n    volumes:\n      - postgres-data:/var/lib/postgresql/data\n    restart: unless-stopped\n    networks:\n      - sentinel-net\n\n  redis:\n    image: redis:7-alpine\n    container_name: vsentinel-redis\n    command: redis-server --requirepass ${REDIS_PASSWORD}\n    volumes:\n      - redis-data:/data\n    restart: unless-stopped\n    networks:\n      - sentinel-net\n\n  nginx:\n    image: nginx:alpine\n    container_name: vsentinel-nginx\n    ports:\n      - "80:80"\n      - "443:443"\n    volumes:\n      - ./nginx/nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf:ro\n      - ./nginx/ssl:/etc/nginx/ssl:ro\n    depends_on:\n      - sentinel\n    restart: unless-stopped\n    networks:\n      - sentinel-net\n\nvolumes:\n  postgres-data:\n  redis-data:\n\nnetworks:\n  sentinel-net:\n    driver: bridge\n```\n\n---\n\n## Kubernetes Deployment\n\n### Prerequisites\n\n- Kubernetes cluster (1.24+)\n- kubectl configured\n- Helm 3.0+\n\n### Using Helm\n\n1. **Add the V-Sentinel Helm repository:**\n```bash\nhelm repo add vsentinel https://charts.v-sentinel.io\nhelm repo update\n```\n\n2. **Install V-Sentinel:**\n```bash\nhelm install vsentinel vsentinel/vsentinel \\\n  --namespace vsentinel \\\n  --create-namespace \\\n  --set config.database.url="postgresql://..." \\\n  --set config.redis.url="redis://..."\n```\n\n3. **Upgrade V-Sentinel:**\n```bash\nhelm upgrade vsentinel vsentinel/vsentinel \\\n  --namespace vsentinel \\\n  --values custom-values.yaml\n```\n\n### Manual Kubernetes Deployment\n\n#### Namespace\n```yaml\napiVersion: v1\nkind: Namespace\nmetadata:\n  name: vsentinel\n```\n\n#### ConfigMap\n```yaml\napiVersion: v1\nkind: ConfigMap\nmetadata:\n  name: vsentinel-config\n  namespace: vsentinel\ndata:\n  sentinel.toml: |\n    [server]\n    address = "0.0.0.0:8080"\n    \n    [database]\n    url = "postgresql://vsentinel:password@postgres:5432/vsentinel"\n    \n    [redis]\n    url = "redis://:password@redis:6379"\n    \n    [security]\n    level = "high"\n```\n\n#### Secret\n```yaml\napiVersion: v1\nkind: Secret\nmetadata:\n  name: vsentinel-secrets\n  namespace: vsentinel\ntype: Opaque\ndata:\n  db-password: <base64-encoded-password>\n  redis-password: <base64-encoded-password>\n  api-key: <base64-encoded-api-key>\n```\n\n#### Deployment\n```yaml\napiVersion: apps/v1\nkind: Deployment\nmetadata:\n  name: vsentinel\n  namespace: vsentinel\nspec:\n  replicas: 3\n  selector:\n    matchLabels:\n      app: vsentinel\n  template:\n    metadata:\n      labels:\n        app: vsentinel\n    spec:\n      containers:\n      - name: vsentinel\n        image: vantis/vsentinel:latest\n        ports:\n        - containerPort: 8080\n        env:\n        - name: RUST_LOG\n          value: "info"\n        - name: SENTINEL_CONFIG\n          value: "/config/sentinel.toml"\n        volumeMounts:\n        - name: config\n          mountPath: /config\n          readOnly: true\n        - name: secrets\n          mountPath: /secrets\n          readOnly: true\n        resources:\n          requests:\n            memory: "512Mi"\n            cpu: "500m"\n          limits:\n            memory: "2Gi"\n            cpu: "2000m"\n        livenessProbe:\n          httpGet:\n            path: /health\n            port: 8080\n          initialDelaySeconds: 30\n          periodSeconds: 10\n        readinessProbe:\n          httpGet:\n            path: /ready\n            port: 8080\n          initialDelaySeconds: 10\n          periodSeconds: 5\n      volumes:\n      - name: config\n        configMap:\n          name: vsentinel-config\n      - name: secrets\n        secret:\n          secretName: vsentinel-secrets\n```\n\n#### Service\n```yaml\napiVersion: v1\nkind: Service\nmetadata:\n  name: vsentinel\n  namespace: vsentinel\nspec:\n  selector:\n    app: vsentinel\n  ports:\n  - port: 80\n    targetPort: 8080\n    name: http\n  type: ClusterIP\n```\n\n#### Ingress\n```yaml\napiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1\nkind: Ingress\nmetadata:\n  name: vsentinel-ingress\n  namespace: vsentinel\n  annotations:\n    cert-manager.io/cluster-issuer: letsencrypt-prod\n    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/ssl-redirect: "true"\nspec:\n  tls:\n  - hosts:\n    - sentinel.example.com\n    secretName: vsentinel-tls\n  rules:\n  - host: sentinel.example.com\n    http:\n      paths:\n      - path: /\n        pathType: Prefix\n        backend:\n          service:\n            name: vsentinel\n            port:\n              number: 80\n```\n\n### HorizontalPodAutoscaler\n\n```yaml\napiVersion: autoscaling/v2\nkind: HorizontalPodAutoscaler\nmetadata:\n  name: vsentinel-hpa\n  namespace: vsentinel\nspec:\n  scaleTargetRef:\n    apiVersion: apps/v1\n    kind: Deployment\n    name: vsentinel\n  minReplicas: 3\n  maxReplicas: 10\n  metrics:\n  - type: Resource\n    resource:\n      name: cpu\n      target:\n        type: Utilization\n        averageUtilization: 70\n  - type: Resource\n    resource:\n      name: memory\n      target:\n        type: Utilization\n        averageUtilization: 80\n```\n\n---\n\n## Bare Metal Deployment\n\n### System Setup\n\n1. **Update system:**\n```bash\napt update && apt upgrade -y\n```\n\n2. **Install dependencies:**\n```bash\napt install -y \\\n    build-essential \\\n    pkg-config \\\n    libssl-dev \\\n    postgresql-client \\\n    redis-tools \\\n    nginx \\\n    certbot\n```\n\n3. **Install Rust:**\n```bash\ncurl --proto \'=https\' --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh\nsource $HOME/.cargo/env\n```\n\n4. **Build V-Sentinel:**\n```bash\ngit clone https://github.com/vantisCorp/V-Sentinel.git\ncd V-Sentinel\ncargo build --release\n```\n\n### Service Configuration\n\nCreate a systemd service file:\n\n```ini\n[Unit]\nDescription=V-Sentinel Security System\nAfter=network.target postgresql.service redis.service\n\n[Service]\nType=simple\nUser=vsentinel\nGroup=vsentinel\nWorkingDirectory=/opt/vsentinel\nExecStart=/opt/vsentinel/target/release/sentinel\nRestart=always\nRestartSec=10\nEnvironment="RUST_LOG=info"\nEnvironment="SENTINEL_CONFIG=/etc/vsentinel/sentinel.toml"\n\n# Security\nNoNewPrivileges=true\nPrivateTmp=true\nProtectSystem=strict\nProtectHome=true\nReadWritePaths=/var/lib/vsentinel /var/log/vsentinel\n\n# Resource limits\nLimitNOFILE=65536\nLimitNPROC=4096\n\n[Install]\nWantedBy=multi-user.target\n```\n\nEnable and start the service:\n\n```bash\nsystemctl enable vsentinel\nsystemctl start vsentinel\nsystemctl status vsentinel\n```\n\n---\n\n## Configuration\n\n### Configuration File (`sentinel.toml`)\n\n```toml\n[server]\naddress = "0.0.0.0:8080"\ntls_address = "0.0.0.0:8443"\ntls_cert = "/etc/vsentinel/cert.pem"\ntls_key = "/etc/vsentinel/key.pem"\n\n[database]\nurl = "postgresql://vsentinel:password@localhost:5432/vsentinel"\nmax_connections = 100\nmin_connections = 10\n\n[redis]\nurl = "redis://:password@localhost:6379/0"\nmax_connections = 50\n\n[security]\nlevel = "high"\nenable_encryption = true\nenable_audit_log = true\nsession_timeout = 3600\n\n[privacy]\nenable_zkp = true\nzkp_backend = "bulletproofs"\ndp_epsilon = 1.0\n\n[quantum]\nalgorithm = "crystals-kyber"\nkey_rotation_interval = 86400\n\n[ai]\nmodel_path = "/models"\ninference_threads = 4\nenable_federated_learning = true\n\n[monitoring]\nenable_metrics = true\nmetrics_port = 9090\nenable_tracing = true\n\n[logging]\nlevel = "info"\nformat = "json"\noutput = "both"\nfile = "/var/log/vsentinel/sentinel.log"\n```\n\n### Environment Variables\n\n```bash\n# Server\nSENTINEL_SERVER_ADDRESS=0.0.0.0:8080\nSENTINEL_TLS_ADDRESS=0.0.0.0:8443\n\n# Database\nDATABASE_URL=postgresql://vsentinel:password@localhost:5432/vsentinel\nDATABASE_MAX_CONNECTIONS=100\n\n# Redis\nREDIS_URL=redis://:password@localhost:6379/0\n\n# Security\nSENTINEL_SECURITY_LEVEL=high\nSENTINEL_API_KEY=your-api-key\n\n# Logging\nRUST_LOG=info\n```\n\n---\n\n## Monitoring\n\n### Prometheus Metrics\n\nV-Sentinel exposes Prometheus metrics on port 9090:\n\n```yaml\nscrape_configs:\n  - job_name: \'vsentinel\'\n    static_configs:\n      - targets: [\'localhost:9090\']\n    metrics_path: /metrics\n```\n\n### Grafana Dashboard\n\nImport the V-Sentinel dashboard for monitoring:\n\n1. Install Grafana\n2. Add Prometheus data source\n3. Import dashboard ID: `12345` (V-Sentinel)\n\n### Key Metrics to Monitor\n\n| Metric | Description | Threshold |\n|--------|-------------|-----------|\n| `sentinel_requests_total` | Total requests | - |\n| `sentinel_request_duration` | Request duration | < 100ms p95 |\n| `sentinel_threats_blocked` | Threats blocked | - |\n| `sentinel_security_score` | Security score | > 95% |\n| `sentinel_cpu_usage` | CPU usage | < 70% |\n| `sentinel_memory_usage` | Memory usage | < 80% |\n\n### Alerting Rules\n\n```yaml\ngroups:\n  - name: vsentinel\n    rules:\n      - alert: HighSecurityThreatLevel\n        expr: sentinel_threat_level > 0.8\n        for: 5m\n        labels:\n          severity: critical\n        annotations:\n          summary: "High security threat level detected"\n          \n      - alert: HighErrorRate\n        expr: rate(sentinel_errors_total[5m]) > 0.1\n        for: 5m\n        labels:\n          severity: warning\n        annotations:\n          summary: "High error rate detected"\n          \n      - alert: ServiceDown\n        expr: up{job="vsentinel"} == 0\n        for: 1m\n        labels:\n          severity: critical\n        annotations:\n          summary: "V-Sentinel service is down"\n```\n\n---\n\n## Security Hardening\n\n### TLS Configuration\n\n```nginx\nserver {\n    listen 443 ssl http2;\n    server_name sentinel.example.com;\n\n    ssl_certificate /etc/nginx/ssl/cert.pem;\n    ssl_certificate_key /etc/nginx/ssl/key.pem;\n\n    ssl_protocols TLSv1.2 TLSv1.3;\n    ssl_ciphers ECDHE-RSA-AES256-GCM-SHA512:DHE-RSA-AES256-GCM-SHA512;\n    ssl_prefer_server_ciphers off;\n    ssl_session_cache shared:SSL:10m;\n    ssl_session_timeout 10m;\n\n    location / {\n        proxy_pass http://localhost:8080;\n        proxy_set_header Host $host;\n        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;\n        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;\n        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Firewall Rules\n\n```bash\n# Allow SSH\nufw allow 22/tcp\n\n# Allow HTTP/HTTPS\nufw allow 80/tcp\nufw allow 443/tcp\n\n# Allow V-Sentinel ports\nufw allow 8080/tcp\nufw allow 8443/tcp\n\n# Enable firewall\nufw enable\n```\n\n### Rate Limiting\n\n```nginx\nhttp {\n    limit_req_zone $binary_remote_addr zone=sentinel_limit:10m rate=10r/s;\n    \n    server {\n        location /api/ {\n            limit_req zone=sentinel_limit burst=20 nodelay;\n            proxy_pass http://localhost:8080;\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Common Issues\n\n#### Service Won\'t Start\n\n```bash\n# Check logs\njournalctl -u vsentinel -n 100\n\n# Check configuration\nsentinel --check-config\n\n# Check dependencies\nsystemctl status postgresql\nsystemctl status redis\n```\n\n#### High Memory Usage\n\n```bash\n# Check memory usage\nfree -h\n\n# Check process memory\nps aux | grep sentinel\n\n# Restart service\nsystemctl restart vsentinel\n```\n\n#### Database Connection Issues\n\n```bash\n# Test database connection\npsql -U vsentinel -h localhost -d vsentinel\n\n# Check connection count\npsql -U vsentinel -h localhost -d vsentinel -c "SELECT count(*) FROM pg_stat_activity;"\n```\n\n### Health Checks\n\n```bash\n# Health check endpoint\ncurl http://localhost:8080/health\n\n# Ready check\ncurl http://localhost:8080/ready\n\n# Metrics endpoint\ncurl http://localhost:9090/metrics\n```\n\n### Logs\n\n```bash\n# Application logs\ntail -f /var/log/vsentinel/sentinel.log\n\n# System logs\njournalctl -u vsentinel -f\n\n# Docker logs\ndocker-compose logs -f sentinel\n```\n\n---\n\n## Backup and Recovery\n\n### Database Backup\n\n```bash\n# Backup\npg_dump -U vsentinel vsentinel > backup_$(date +%Y%m%d).sql\n\n# Restore\npsql -U vsentinel vsentinel < backup_20240304.sql\n```\n\n### Configuration Backup\n\n```bash\n# Backup configuration\ntar -czf config_backup_$(date +%Y%m%d).tar.gz /etc/vsentinel\n\n# Restore\ntar -xzf config_backup_20240304.tar.gz -C /\n```\n\n---\n\n## Support\n\nFor additional support:\n- Documentation: Please install Rust.${NC}"\n        exit 1\n    fi\n    \n    # Build benchmarks first\n    echo -e "${YELLOW}Building benchmarks...${NC}"\n    cargo build --release --benches\n    \n    echo ""\n    echo -e "${BLUE}Running benchmarks by module...${NC}"\n    echo ""\n    \n    # Run all benchmark groups\n    run_module_benchmark "privacy"\n    run_module_benchmark "quantum"\n    run_module_benchmark "biometrics"\n    run_module_benchmark "neural"\n    run_module_benchmark "autonomous"\n    run_module_benchmark "metaverse"\n    run_module_benchmark "blockchain"\n    run_module_benchmark "siem"\n    run_module_benchmark "core"\n    \n    # Compare thresholds\n    compare_thresholds\n    \n    # Generate summary\n    echo -e "${BLUE}======================================${NC}"\n    echo -e "${BLUE}  Benchmark Summary${NC}"\n    echo -e "${BLUE}======================================${NC}"\n    echo ""\n    \n    echo "Results saved to: ${RESULTS_FILE}"\n    echo "Thresholds file: ${THRESHOLDS_FILE}"\n    echo ""\n    \n    # Generate HTML report if available\n    if [ -d "target/criterion" ]; then\n        echo -e "${GREEN}HTML reports available at: target/criterion/reports/${NC}"\n    fi\n    \n    echo -e "${GREEN}Benchmark suite completed!${NC}"\n}\n\n# Run main\nmain "$@"\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

value\n\n        return thresholds\n\n    def generate_summary(self, results: Dict, thresholds: Dict) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Generate performance summary with pass/fail status."""\n }\n\n        for bench_name, data in results.items():\n            mean_ms = data.get("mean_ns", 0) / 1_000_000  # ns to ms\n            std_dev_ms = data.get("std_dev_ns", 0) / 1_000_000\n\n            # Check against threshold (simplified)\n            status = "passed"  # Default to passed\n            threshold = None\n\n            # Look for matching threshold\n            for section, thresh_data in thresholds.items():\n                for key, value in thresh_data.items():\n                    if key.replace("_ms", "") in bench_name.lower() and isinstance(value, (int, float)):\n                        threshold = value\n                        status = "passed" if mean_ms <= value else "failed"\n                        break\n                if threshold:\n                    break\n\n            if status == "passed":\n                summary["passed"] += 1\n            else:\n                summary["failed"] += 1\n\n            summary["modules"][bench_name] = {\n                "mean_ms": round(mean_ms, 4),\n                "std_dev_ms": round(std_dev_ms, 4),\n                "threshold_ms": threshold,\n                "status": status\n            }\n\n        return summary\n\n    def generate_html_report(self, summary: Dict) -> str:\n        """Generate HTML performance report."""\n        html = f\'\'\'<!DOCTYPE html>\n<html lang="en">\n<head>\n    <meta Let me create security audit documentation and tools:\n\n<function_calls><create-file file_path="scripts/security_audit.sh">\n#!/bin/bash\n#\n# V-Sentinel Security Audit Script\n#\n# Automated security audit and vulnerability scanning\n\nset -e\n\n# Colors\nRED=\'\\033[0;31m\'\nGREEN=\'\\033[0;32m\'\nYELLOW=\'\\033[1;33m\'\nBLUE=\'\\033[0;34m\'\nNC=\'\\033[0m\'\n\n# Configuration\nREPORTS_DIR="security_reports"\nTIMESTAMP=$(date +"%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")\nREPORT_FILE="${REPORTS_DIR}/audit_${TIMESTAMP}.md"\n\n# Create reports directory\nmkdir -p "${REPORTS_DIR}"\n\n# Functions\nlog_info() {\n    echo -e "${BLUE}[INFO]${NC} $1"\n}\n\nlog_success() {\n    echo -e "${GREEN}[SUCCESS]${NC} $1"\n}\n\nlog_warning() {\n    echo -e "${YELLOW}[WARNING]${NC} $1"\n}\n\nlog_error() {\n    echo -e "${RED}[ERROR]${NC} $1"\n}\n\n# Initialize report\ninit_report() {\n    cat > "${REPORT_FILE}" << EOF\n# V-Sentinel Security Audit Report\n\n**Date:** $(date +"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")\n**Auditor:** Automated Security Audit\n**Version:** 1.0.0\n\n---\n\n## Executive Summary\n\nThis report contains the results of the automated security audit for V-Sentinel.\n\n---\n\n## 1. Code Security Analysis\n\nEOF\n}\n\n# Check for hardcoded secrets\ncheck_secrets() {\n    log_info "Checking for hardcoded secrets..."\n    \n    local findings=0\n    local output_file="${REPORTS_DIR}/secrets_${TIMESTAMP}.txt"\n    \n    # Check for potential secrets\n    grep -rn --include="*.rs" --include="*.toml" --include="*.yaml" --include="*.json" \\\n        -E "(password|secret|api_key|token|private_key)\\s*=\\s*[\\"\'][^\\"\']+[\\"\']" \\\n        . 2>/dev/null | grep -v ".git" | grep -v "example" | grep -v "test" > "${output_file}" || true\n    \n    findings=$(wc -l < "${output_file}")\n    \n    echo "### 1.1 Hardcoded Secrets Check" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    echo "" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    \n    if [ "$findings" -gt 0 ]; then\n        echo "⚠️ **Potential hardcoded secrets found: ${findings}**" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        echo "" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        echo "\\`\\`\\`" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        head -20 "${output_file}" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        echo "\\`\\`\\`" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        log_warning "Found ${findings} potential hardcoded secrets"\n    else\n        echo "✅ **No hardcoded secrets detected**" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        log_success "No hardcoded secrets found"\n    fi\n    \n    echo "" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n}\n\n# Check dependencies for vulnerabilities\ncheck_dependencies() {\n    log_info "Checking dependencies for vulnerabilities..."\n    \n    echo "### 1.2 Dependency Vulnerability Check" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    echo "" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    \n    if [ -f "Cargo.lock" ]; then\n        # Run cargo audit if available\n        if command -v cargo-audit &> /dev/null; then\n            cargo audit > "${REPORTS_DIR}/cargo_audit_${TIMESTAMP}.txt" 2>&1 || true\n            if grep -q "No known security vulnerabilities" "${REPORTS_DIR}/cargo_audit_${TIMESTAMP}.txt"; then\n                echo "✅ **No vulnerable dependencies found**" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n                log_success "No vulnerable dependencies"\n            else\n                echo "⚠️ **Vulnerable dependencies found**" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n                echo "" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n                echo "\\`\\`\\`" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n                cat "${REPORTS_DIR}/cargo_audit_${TIMESTAMP}.txt" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n                echo "\\`\\`\\`" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n                log_warning "Vulnerable dependencies found"\n            fi\n        else\n            echo "ℹ️ cargo-audit not available, skipping dependency check" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n            log_warning "cargo-audit not installed"\n        fi\n    else\n        echo "ℹ️ Cargo.lock not found, skipping dependency check" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    fi\n    \n    echo "" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n}\n\n# Check for insecure code patterns\ncheck_code_patterns() {\n    log_info "Checking for insecure code patterns..."\n    \n    echo "### 1.3 Insecure Code Pattern Check" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    echo "" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    \n    local findings=0\n    local output_file="${REPORTS_DIR}/patterns_${TIMESTAMP}.txt"\n    \n    # Check for insecure patterns\n    grep -rn --include="*.rs" \\\n        -E "(unwrap\\(\\)|expect\\(\\)|panic!|unsafe)" \\\n        src/ 2>/dev/null > "${output_file}" || true\n    \n    findings=$(wc -l < "${output_file}")\n    \n    echo "Found ${findings} potentially unsafe code patterns:" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    echo "" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    echo "- unwrap() calls: $(grep -c "unwrap()" "${output_file}" || echo 0)" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    echo "- expect() calls: $(grep -c "expect(" "${output_file}" || echo 0)" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    echo "- panic! macros: $(grep -c "panic!" "${output_file}" || echo 0)" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    echo "- unsafe blocks: $(grep -c "unsafe" "${output_file}" || echo 0)" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    \n    log_info "Found ${findings} potentially unsafe patterns"\n    \n    echo "" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n}\n\n# Check file permissions\ncheck_permissions() {\n    log_info "Checking file permissions..."\n    \n    echo "### 1.4 File Permission Check" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    echo "" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    \n    local issues=0\n    \n    # Check for world-writable files\n    local writable=$(find . -type f -perm -002 -not -path "./.git/*" 2>/dev/null | wc -l)\n    \n    if [ "$writable" -gt 0 ]; then\n        echo "⚠️ Found ${writable} world-writable files" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        issues=$((issues + writable))\n    else\n        echo "✅ No world-writable files found" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    fi\n    \n    # Check for sensitive files with loose permissions\n    if [ -f "config/sentinel.toml" ]; then\n        local config_perms=$(stat -c %a config/sentinel.toml 2>/dev/null || echo "644")\n        echo "Configuration file permissions: ${config_perms}" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    fi\n    \n    log_info "File permission check completed"\n    \n    echo "" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n}\n\n# Check SSL/TLS configuration\ncheck_ssl_tls() {\n    log_info "Checking SSL/TLS configuration..."\n    \n    echo "### 1.5 SSL/TLS Configuration Check" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    echo "" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    \n    if [ -f "deploy/nginx/nginx.conf" ]; then\n        local ssl_protocols=$(grep -E "ssl_protocols" deploy/nginx/nginx.conf || echo "Not found")\n        local ssl_ciphers=$(grep -E "ssl_ciphers" deploy/nginx/nginx.conf || echo "Not found")\n        \n        echo "**Configured SSL Protocols:**" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        echo "\\`\\`\\`" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        echo "${ssl_protocols}" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        echo "\\`\\`\\`" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        echo "" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        \n        echo "**Configured Cipher Suites:**" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        echo "\\`\\`\\`" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        echo "${ssl_ciphers}" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        echo "\\`\\`\\`" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        \n        # Check for insecure protocols\n        if echo "${ssl_protocols}" | grep -qE "(SSLv2|SSLv3|TLSv1[^\\.])"; then\n            echo "⚠️ Insecure SSL/TLS protocols detected" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n            log_warning "Insecure SSL/TLS protocols found"\n        else\n            echo "✅ SSL/TLS configuration appears secure" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n            log_success "SSL/TLS configuration is secure"\n        fi\n    else\n        echo "ℹ️ NGINX configuration not found" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    fi\n    \n    echo "" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n}\n\n# Check API security\ncheck_api_security() {\n    log_info "Checking API security..."\n    \n    echo "### 1.6 API Security Check" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    echo "" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n    \n    if [ -f "docs/API_DOCUMENTATION.md" ]; then\n        # Check for authentication requirements\n        if grep -q "Authorization: Bearer" docs/API_DOCUMENTATION.md; then\n            echo "✅ API endpoints require authentication" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        else\n            echo "⚠️ Some API endpoints may not require authentication" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        fi\n        \n        # Check for rate limiting\n        if grep -q "rate" docs/API_DOCUMENTATION.md; then\n            echo "✅ Rate limiting is documented" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        else\n            echo "⚠️ Rate limiting documentation not found" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        fi\n    fi\n    \n    # Check NGINX rate limiting configuration\n    if [ -f "deploy/nginx/nginx.conf" ]; then\n        if grep -q "limit_req_zone" deploy/nginx/nginx.conf; then\n            echo "✅ Rate limiting is configured in NGINX" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        fi\n        \n        if grep -q "limit_conn_zone" deploy/nginx/nginx.conf; then\n            echo "✅ Connection limiting is configured in NGINX" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n        fi\n    fi\n    \n    log_info "API security check completed"\n    \n    echo "" >> "${REPORT_FILE}"\n}\n\n# Generate summary\ngenerate_summary() {\n    log_info "Generating audit summary..."\n    \n    cat >> "${REPORT_FILE}" << EOF\n\n---\n\n## 2. Security Recommendations\n\nBased on the audit findings, the following recommendations are provided:\n\n### 2.1 Immediate Actions\n- Review all hardcoded secrets and move to environment variables\n- Update vulnerable dependencies\n- Fix insecure code patterns (unwrap, expect, unsafe)\n\n### 2.2 Short-term Actions\n- Implement automated dependency scanning in CI/CD\n- Add security linters to development workflow\n- Review and update cryptographic configurations\n\n### 2.3 Long-term Actions\n- Conduct regular penetration testing\n- Implement security monitoring and alerting\n- Establish security incident response procedures\n\n---\n\n## 3. Compliance Checklist\n\n- [ ] OWASP Top 10 reviewed\n- [ ] Security headers implemented\n- [ ] Authentication mechanisms verified\n- [ ] Authorization controls tested\n- [ ] Input validation implemented\n- [ ] Output encoding implemented\n- [ ] Error handling secure\n- [ ] Logging and monitoring configured\n- [ ] Data protection measures in place\n- [ ] Cryptographic standards verified\n\n---\n\n## 4. Audit Trail\n\n| Check | Status | Findings |\n|-------|--------|----------|\n| Hardcoded Secrets | Completed | See report |\n| Dependency Vulnerabilities | Completed | See report |\n| Insecure Patterns | Completed | See report |\n| File Permissions | Completed | See report |\n| SSL/TLS Config | Completed | See report |\n| API Security | Completed | See report |\n\n---\n\n**Report Generated:** $(date +"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")\n**Next Audit Recommended:** $(date -d "+30 days" +"%Y-%m-%d" 2>/dev/null || date -v+30d +"%Y-%m-%d" 2>/dev/null || echo "In 30 days")\n\nEOF\n\n    log_success "Audit report saved to: ${REPORT_FILE}"\n}\n\n# Main execution\nmain() {\n    echo -e "${BLUE}======================================${NC}"\n    echo -e "${BLUE}  V-Sentinel Security Audit${NC}"\n    echo -e "${BLUE}======================================${NC}"\n    echo ""\n    \n    init_report\n    check_secrets\n    check_dependencies\n    check_code_patterns\n    check_permissions\n    check_ssl_tls\n    check_api_security\n    generate_summary\n    \n    echo ""\n    echo -e "${GREEN}Security audit completed!${NC}"\n    echo -e "Report: ${REPORT_FILE}"\n}\n\nmain "$@"\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

  configs: HashMap<String, PluginConfig>,\n}\n\nimpl PluginRegistry {\n    /// Create a new plugin registry\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            plugins: HashMap::new(),\n            configs: HashMap::new(),\n        }\n    }\n    \n    /// Register a plugin\n    pub fn register<P: Plugin + \'static>(&mut self, plugin: P, config: PluginConfig) -> Result<(), PluginError> {\n        let metadata = plugin.metadata();\n        let plugin_id = metadata.id.clone();\n        \n        // Validate dependencies\n        self.validate_dependencies(&metadata.dependencies)?;\n        \n        // Store config\n        self.configs.insert(plugin_id.clone(), config);\n        \n        // Store plugin\n        self.plugins.insert(plugin_id, Box::new(plugin));\n        \n        Ok(())\n    }\n    \n    /// Unregister a plugin\n    pub fn unregister(&mut self, plugin_id: &str) -> Result<(), PluginError> {\n        if self.plugins.remove(plugin_id).is_none() {\n            return Err(PluginError::NotFound(plugin_id.to_string()));\n        }\n        self.configs.remove(plugin_id);\n        Ok(())\n    }\n    \n    /// Get a plugin by ID\n    pub fn get(&self, plugin_id: &str) -> Option<&dyn Plugin> {\n        self.plugins.get(plugin_id).map(|p| p.as_ref())\n    }\n    \n    /// List all registered plugins\n    pub fn list(&self) -> Vec<&PluginMetadata> {\n        self.plugins.values().map(|p| p.metadata()).collect()\n    }\n    \n    /// Initialize all plugins\n    pub async fn initialize_all(&mut self) -> Result<(), PluginError> {\n        for (plugin_id, plugin) in &mut self.plugins {\n            let config = self.configs.get(plugin_id).cloned().unwrap_or_default();\n            plugin.initialize(config).await?;\n        }\n        Ok(())\n    }\n    \n    /// Shutdown all plugins\n    pub async fn shutdown_all(&mut self) -> Result<(), PluginError> {\n        for plugin in self.plugins.values_mut() {\n            plugin.shutdown().await?;\n        }\n        Ok(())\n    }\n    \n    /// Validate plugin dependencies\n    fn validate_dependencies(&self, dependencies: &[PluginDependency]) -> Result<(), PluginError> {\n        for dep in dependencies {\n            if !dep.optional && !self.plugins.contains_key(&dep.plugin_id) {\n                return Err(PluginError::DependencyNotMet(format!(\n                    "Required   let (event_tx, _) = tokio::sync::broadcast::channel(1000);\n        Self {\n            registry: Arc::new(tokio::sync::RwLock::new(PluginRegistry::new())),\n            event_tx,\n        }\n    }\n    \n    /// Register a plugin\n    pub async fn register<P: Plugin + \'static>(&self, plugin: P, config: PluginConfig) -> Result<(), PluginError> {\n        let mut registry = &PluginContext) -> Result<(), PluginError> {\n        // Broadcast event\n        let _ = self.event_tx.send(event.clone());\n        \n        // Process with plugins\n        let registry = self.registry.read().await;\n        for plugin in registry.plugins.values() {\n            if let Err(e) = plugin.handle_event(event, context).await {\n                tracing::warn!("Plugin event handling failed: {}", e);\n            }\n        }\n        \n        Ok(())\n    }\n    \n    /// Execute a command on a specific plugin\n    pub async fn execute_command(&self, plugin_id: &str, registry.plugins.get(plugin_id).ok_or_else(|| PluginError::NotFound(plugin_id.to_string()))?;\n        plugin.execute(command, args, context).await\n    }\n    \n    /// Get plugin health\n    pub fn get_all_health(&self) -> HashMap<String, PluginHealth> {\n        let registry = self.registry.read().await;\n        let mut health = HashMap::new();\n        for (id, plugin) in &registry.plugins {\n            if let Ok(h) = plugin.health_check().await {\n                health.insert(id.clone(), h);\n            }\n        }\n        health\n    }\n    \n    /// Subscribe to events\n    pub fn subscribe(&self) -> tokio::sync::broadcast::Receiver<PluginEvent> {\n        self.event_tx.subscribe()\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Default for PluginManager {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self::new()\n    }\n}\n\n// ============================================================================\n// Example Plugin Implementation\n// Lifecycle\n\n1. **Registration** - Plugin is registered with the plugin manager\n2. **Initialization** - Plugin is initialized with configuration\n3. **Execution** - Plugin handles events and `UserAction` | User action event |\n| `SystemEvent` | System event |\n| `Custom(String)` | Custom event type |\n\n## Best Practices\n\n1. **Minimal Permissions** - Request only the permissions your plugin needs\n2. **Error Handling** - Handle all errors gracefully\n3. **Logging** - Use tracing for plugin logs\n4. **Configuration** - Make your plugin configurable\n5. **Testing** - Write comprehensive tests\n6. **Documentation** - Document all commands and events\n7. **Performance** - Keep execution time minimal\n8. **Security** - Validate all inputs\n\n## Plugin
